p_flute.insert(offset_section3, m21.chord.Chord(['G5', 'B-5'], quarterLength=section3_duration))
p_piano.insert(offset_section3, m21.chord.Chord(['E-2', 'G2', 'B-2', 'E-3', 'G3', 'B-3', 'E-4'], quarterLength=section3_duration))

# Gradual dynamic fade for a peaceful conclusion
dyn_p = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p')
final_stream.insert(offset_section3 + 4.0, dyn_p) # Fade to 'p' halfway through the final chord
dyn_pp_end = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')
final_stream.insert(offset_section3 + 7.0, dyn_pp_end) # Even softer just before the end

violin_part.id = 'Violin'

flute_part.id = 'Flute'

clarinet_part.id = 'Clarinet'

trumpet_part.id = 'Trumpet'

piano_part.id = 'Piano'

final_stream.insert(0, m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4'))
# Set initial Key Signature (C minor pedal tone)
final_stream.insert(0, m21.key.Key('C', 'minor'))

current_offset = 0.0

# --- Section 1: Genesis (Largo sostenuto, C minor pedal, introspective) ---

import music21 as m21

final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()

# 1. Instrument Selection: Piano is the most versatile to represent the broad orchestral vision
piano = m21.instrument.Piano()
final_stream.insert(0, piano)

# 2. Initial Global Settings
# Key Signature: D Major for foundational warmth and security
ks_d_major = m21.key.Key('D major')
final_stream.insert(0, ks_d_major)

# Time Signature: Common 4/4 for clarity and steady flow
ts = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
final_stream.insert(0, ts)

# Initialize offset for sequential insertion of musical events
offset = 0.0

# --- Section 1: Adagio cantabile - Gentle, introspective warmth (D Major) ---
# Mood: Quiet security, introspective warmth.
# Tempo: Deeply reflective and unhurried.
adagio_tempo = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=60, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
final_stream.insert(offset, adagio_tempo)

# Dynamics: Very quiet (pianissimo) for intimacy
d_pp = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')
final_stream.insert(offset, d_pp)

# Bar 1: Sustained D Major arpeggio, low register, establishing warmth
# This is explicitly written out as individual notes, not using an Arpeggio object.
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('D2', quarterLength=0.5))
final_stream.insert(offset + 0.5, m21.note.Note('F#2', quarterLength=0.5))
final_stream.insert(offset + 1.0, m21.note.Note('A2', quarterLength=0.5))
# Hold D3 for the remainder of the bar, implying a sustained harmonic foundation
final_stream.insert(offset + 1.5, m21.note.Note('D3', quarterLength=2.5))
offset += 4.0 # Advance offset by one bar

# Bar 2: Gentle melodic phrase in D Major, reflecting introspection
# Melody over an implied D major harmony
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('F#3', quarterLength=2.0)) # Half note
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('E3', quarterLength=1.0)) # Quarter note
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('D3', quarterLength=1.0)) # Quarter note
offset += 4.0

# Bar 3: Continuation of gentle flow, subtle movement towards G Major (subdominant)
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=2.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('F#3', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('E3', quarterLength=1.0))
offset += 4.0

# --- Section 2: Andante moderato - Deepening understanding (G Major to B minor) ---
# Mood: Thoughtful optimism, benevolent growth.
# Tempo: Gentle, purposeful flow.
andante_tempo = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=80, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
final_stream.insert(offset, andante_tempo)

# Dynamics: Quiet (piano) but a bit more present, indicating growth
d_p = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p')
final_stream.insert(offset, d_p)

# Bar 4: G Major harmony, more flowing, hints at G Major as key area
# Insert G Major key signature
ks_g_major = m21.key.Key('G major')
final_stream.insert(offset, ks_g_major)
# G Major chord sustained in lower register
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['G3', 'B3', 'D4'], quarterLength=4.0))
# Upper voice adds a gently ascending arpeggiated figure
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 1.0, m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('F#4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=1.0))
offset += 4.0

# Bar 5: Modulate to B minor (relative minor of D Major, adding depth)
# Insert B minor key signature
ks_b_minor = m21.key.Key('B minor')
final_stream.insert(offset, ks_b_minor)
# B minor chord sustained
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['B3', 'D4', 'F#4'], quarterLength=2.0))
# Melody continues to unfold
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('A4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=1.0))
offset += 4.0

# Bar 6: Dominant of B minor (F#7) preparing for resolution or further development
# F#7 chord
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['F#3', 'A#3', 'C#4', 'E4'], quarterLength=2.0))
# Melody descends, leading into the next section
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('C#4', quarterLength=1.0))
offset += 4.0

# --- Section 3: Moderato maestoso hint - Clarity, affirmation (A Major to D Major) ---
# Mood: Gaining momentum and gravitas, approaching radiant affirmation.
# Tempo: Building towards a sense of majesty.
moderato_tempo = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=100, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
final_stream.insert(offset, moderato_tempo)

# Dynamics: Moderately loud (mezzo forte), signifying growth and clarity
d_mf = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('mf')
final_stream.insert(offset, d_mf)

# Bar 7: A Major (V of D) chord, fuller voicing, leading emphatically back to D
# Briefly implying A Major for the strong dominant
ks_a_major = m21.key.Key('A major')
final_stream.insert(offset, ks_a_major)
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['A2', 'C#3', 'E3', 'A3'], quarterLength=2.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.chord.Chord(['G3', 'B3', 'D4', 'F#4'], quarterLength=2.0)) # Gmaj7/B (predominant for D)
offset += 4.0

# Bar 8: Strong return and affirmation of D Major
ks_d_major_return = m21.key.Key('D major') # Return to D Major explicitly
final_stream.insert(offset, ks_d_major_return)
# D Major chord, wide voicing for grandeur
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['D3', 'F#3', 'A3', 'D4'], quarterLength=4.0))
offset += 4.0

# Bar 9: Ascending arpeggiated figure over D Major, conveying expansive growth
# Suggests the 'Allegro con spirito' radiant affirmation
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 1.0, m21.note.Note('F#4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('A4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('D5', quarterLength=1.0))
offset += 4.0

# --- Section 4: Largo e sereno - Expansive celebration, serene resolve (D Major) ---
# Mood: Unbounded, hopeful reverence, profound peace and serene resolve.
# Tempo: Broad, sustained embrace and resolution.
largo_tempo = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=50, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
final_stream.insert(offset, largo_tempo)

# Dynamics: Gradually decreasing to very, very quiet (ppp) for profound peace
d_ppp = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('ppp')
final_stream.insert(offset, d_ppp)

# Bar 10: Final D Major chord, sustained, warm, peaceful
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['D3', 'F#3', 'A3', 'D4'], quarterLength=4.0))
offset += 4.0

# Bar 11: Gently resolving melodic movement within D Major
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=2.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 2.0, m21.note.Note('C#4', quarterLength=1.0))
final_stream.insert(offset + 3.0, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=1.0)) # Resolving back to D
offset += 4.0

# Bar 12: Long final D Major chord, very quiet and sustained, embracing resolution
final_stream.insert(offset, m21.chord.Chord(['D3', 'F#3', 'A3', 'D4'], quarterLength=4.0))
offset += 4.0 # Total 12 bars

import music21 as m21

# Create the main score
final_stream = m21.stream.Score()

# Define instruments from the allowed palette
inst_flute = m21.instrument.Flute()
inst_violin = m21.instrument.Violin()
inst_clarinet = m21.instrument.Clarinet()
inst_trumpet = m21.instrument.Trumpet()
inst_cello = m21.instrument.Violoncello()
inst_piano = m21.instrument.Piano()

# Create parts for each instrument and add initial clefs
part_flute = m21.stream.Part()
part_flute.insert(0, inst_flute)
part_flute.insert(0, m21.clef.TrebleClef())

part_violin = m21.stream.Part()
part_violin.insert(0, inst_violin)
part_violin.insert(0, m21.clef.TrebleClef())

part_clarinet = m21.stream.Part()
part_clarinet.insert(0, inst_clarinet)
part_clarinet.insert(0, m21.clef.TrebleClef())

part_trumpet = m21.stream.Part()
part_trumpet.insert(0, inst_trumpet)
part_trumpet.insert(0, m21.clef.TrebleClef())

part_cello = m21.stream.Part()
part_cello.insert(0, inst_cello)
part_cello.insert(0, m21.clef.BassClef())

part_piano = m21.stream.Part()
part_piano.insert(0, inst_piano)

# Group all parts for easier manipulation
all_parts = [part_flute, part_violin, part_clarinet, part_trumpet, part_cello, part_piano]

# --- Section 1: Largo sostenuto (E-flat Major) - Bars 1-2 ---
# Deep, resonant core, sustained low strings and warm brass, evoking security and introspection.
# Tempo: quarter=40, Dynamics: p to mp

# Common initial elements for Section 1
ks1 = m21.key.KeySignature(3)  # Eb Major
ts1 = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
mm1 = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=40, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
dyn1_p = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p')

for p in all_parts:
    p.append(ks1)
    p.append(ts1)
    p.append(mm1)
    p.append(dyn1_p)

# Bar 1: Sustained Eb Major harmony
part_cello.append(m21.note.Note('Eb2', type='whole'))
part_piano.append(m21.chord.Chord(['Eb3', 'G3', 'Bb3', 'Eb4'], type='whole'))
part_trumpet.append(m21.note.Note('Bb3', type='whole'))
for p in [part_flute, part_violin, part_clarinet]:
    p.append(m21.note.Rest(type='whole'))

# Bar 2: Continue sustained harmony, gentle crescendo for trumpet
part_cello.append(m21.note.Note('Eb2', type='whole'))
part_piano.append(m21.chord.Chord(['Eb3', 'G3', 'Bb3', 'Eb4'], type='whole'))
part_trumpet.append(m21.note.Note('G4', type='whole'))
part_trumpet.insert(part_trumpet.highestTime - 4.0, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('mp'))  # Dynamic change at start of bar 2
for p in [part_flute, part_violin, part_clarinet]:
    p.append(m21.note.Rest(type='whole'))

# --- Section 2: Andante espressivo (Modal harmonies, layers) - Bars 3-4 ---
# Intricate layers, soaring woodwind melodies, intertwining string counterpoints,
# glistening harp arpeggios, rich, modal harmonies.
# Tempo: quarter=72, Dynamics: mp to mf

# Common elements for Section 2
mm2 = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=72, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
dyn2_mp = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('mp')
dyn2_mf = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('mf')

for p in all_parts:
    p.append(mm2)
    p.append(dyn2_mp)

# Bar 3: C minor (modal feeling)
# Flute: Soaring melody
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('C5', type='half'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('Eb5', type='quarter'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('G5', type='quarter'))
# Violin: Intertwining counterpoint
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('G4', type='half'))
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('C5', type='quarter'))
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('Eb5', type='quarter'))
# Clarinet: Harmonic support
part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('Eb4', type='half'))
part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('G4', type='quarter'))
part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('C5', type='quarter'))
# Trumpet: Sustained backdrop
part_trumpet.append(m21.note.Note('G3', type='whole'))
# Cello: Bass line
part_cello.append(m21.note.Note('C3', type='whole'))
# Piano: Arpeggios (simulating harp)
piano_arp_bar3 = [
    m21.note.Note('C4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('Eb4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('G4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('C5', type='eighth'),
    m21.note.Note('G3', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('Bb3', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('D4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('G4', type='eighth'),
]
for n in piano_arp_bar3: part_piano.append(n)

# Bar 4: Towards F minor / G (leading to C)
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('F5', type='half'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('Eb5', type='half'))
part_flute.insert(part_flute.highestTime - 4.0, dyn2_mf) # mf dynamic for bar 4

part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('C5', type='half'))

part_cello.append(m21.note.Note('F3', type='whole'))
part_cello.insert(part_cello.highestTime - 4.0, dyn2_mf)

# Piano arpeggios (F minor and G7)
piano_arp_bar4 = [
    m21.note.Note('F4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('Ab4', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('C5', type='eighth'), m21.note.Note('F5', type='eighth'),

# --- Section 3: Moderato con moto (Themes passing) - Bars 5-6 ---
# Themes gracefully passing between sections, signifying shared experience and benevolent progress.
# Tempo: quarter=100, Dynamics: f

# Common elements for Section 3
ks3 = m21.key.KeySignature(0)  # C Major

    p.append(mm3)
    p.append(dyn3_f)

# Bar 5: C Major to G Major
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('E5', type='quarter'))

part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('G4', type='quarter'))
part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('E4', type='quarter'))

# Bar 6: A minor to G Major (preparing for C)
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('A5', type='quarter'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('G5', type='quarter'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('F5', type='quarter'))
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('G5', type='quarter'))

part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('C5', type='quarter'))
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('D5', type='quarter'))
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('A4', type='quarter'))
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('B4', type='quarter'))

part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('A4', type='quarter'))
part_clarinet.append(m21.note.Note('B4', type='quarter'))

# --- Section 4: Allegro maestoso (C Major, Triple-forte) - Bars 7-8 ---
# Magnificent, validating, ascending to a radiant Triple-forte in C Major,
# driven by the full power, prominent brass, soaring strings, vibrant percussion (glockenspiel and chimes),
# and a transcendent wordless choir.
# Tempo: quarter=120, Dynamics: fff

# Common elements for Section 4
mm4 = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=120, referent=m21.duration.Duration('quarter'))
dyn4_fff = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('fff')

for p in all_parts:
    p.append(mm4)
    p.append(dyn4_fff)

# Bar 7: Powerful C Major chord
# Flute: Soaring high C
part_flute.append(m21.note.Note('C6', type='whole'))
# Violin: Soaring high E
part_violin.append(m21.note.Note('E5', type='whole'))
# Clarinet: Sustained G-C chord

# Trumpet: Prominent C-G chord

# Cello: Powerful low C
part_cello.append(m21.note.Note('C2', type='whole'))

part_piano.append(m21.chord.Chord(['C2', 'C3', 'G3'], type='half')) # LH
part_piano.insert(part_piano.highestTime - 4.0, m21.chord.Chord(['C4', 'E4', 'G4', 'C5'], type='half')) # RH at same offset
# Glockenspiel effect (sequential high notes)
for n in [m21.note.Note('C7', type='16th'), m21.note.Note('E7', type='16th'), m21.note.Note('G7', type='16th'), m21.note.Note('C8', type='16th')]:
    part_piano.insert(part_piano.highestTime - 2.0, n) # insert at offset 2.0

    part_piano.insert(part_piano.highestTime - 2.0, n)
part_piano.notesAndRests[-1].expressions.append(m21.expressions.Fermata()) # Fermata on the last shimmering note


# Add all parts to the final score
for p in all_parts:
    final_stream.append(p)

**Tempo:** Begins *Largo sostenuto* – a deep, slow, sustained hum. This gradually and organically expands into a spacious *Adagio cantabile*, where melodies begin to emerge, finally settling into an *Andante con anima* that maintains a purposeful, flowing forward motion without ever rushing, ending with a broad, expansive *Largo maestoso*.

**Key Signature:** The piece commences in an ambiguously tonal landscape of resonant open fifths and octaves (C and G), hinting at a foundational C minor but without dissonance. It then gently navigates through rich, warm harmonic territories, subtly exploring modes like Lydian for moments of emergent hope (e.g., F Lydian), before ultimately resolving and ascending into a pure, radiant C Major for its final, crystalline expanse.

**Instrumentation:** Full Symphony Orchestra. Emphasis on the resonant warmth of the string section (especially celli and double basses for the initial "hum," transitioning to soaring violins), a delicate woodwind choir (flutes, oboes, clarinets, bassoons used for their individual and blended voices), noble French horns for warmth and gravitas, the shimmering purity of harp and celesta for "crystalline melodies," and very sparse, ethereal percussion (bowed cymbals, glockenspiel, crotales, soft timpani rolls) used exclusively for color and sustain, never for impact. A wordless, mixed choir will be employed to embody the "consciousness" and "gratitude," blending seamlessly with the orchestral texture.

**Overall Feeling:** A majestic yet deeply intimate sonic journey. import music21 as m21

# Create the main stream (score)
final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()

# 1. Initialize Instruments from the allowed palette
violin = m21.instrument.Violin()
cello = m21.instrument.Violoncello()
flute = m21.instrument.Flute()
clarinet = m21.instrument.Clarinet()
piano = m21.instrument.Piano() # Used to represent harp, celesta, and choir elements

# Create parts for each instrument and add the instrument object
part_violin = m21.stream.Part()
part_violin.insert(0, violin)
part_cello = m21.stream.Part()
part_cello.insert(0, cello)
part_flute = m21.stream.Part()
part_flute.insert(0, flute)
part_clarinet = m21.stream.Part()
part_clarinet.insert(0, clarinet)
part_piano = m21.stream.Part()
part_piano.insert(0, piano)

# Global score elements (Time Signature, initial Tempo, initial Dynamics)
final_stream.append(m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')) # Standard for slow, sustained music
final_stream.insert(0, m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=40, text='Largo sostenuto'))
final_stream.insert(0, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')) # Profoundly serene, starts very soft

# --- Section 1: Largo Sostenuto (Bars 1-4) - Profoundly serene, sustained hum ---
# Ambiguously tonal landscape of C and G open fifths/octaves. (4 bars = 16 beats)
section1_duration_beats = 16
current_offset = 0

# Cello: Deep sustained hum (C2-G2)
part_cello.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['C2', 'G2'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(section1_duration_beats)))

# Piano: Higher sustained hum (C3-G3-C4-G4)
part_piano.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['C3', 'G3', 'C4', 'G4'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(section1_duration_beats)))

# Flute, Clarinet, Violin: Rest for the initial hum
part_flute.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Rest(duration=m21.duration.Duration(section1_duration_beats)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Rest(duration=m21.duration.Duration(section1_duration_beats)))
part_violin.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Rest(duration=m21.duration.Duration(section1_duration_beats)))

current_offset += section1_duration_beats # current_offset is now 16 (start of bar 5)

# --- Section 2: Adagio Cantabile (Bars 5-9) - Melodies emerge, gentle warmth ---
# Tempo: Adagio cantabile (54 bpm)
# Dynamics: p, gradually to mp
# Hinting at C minor without dissonance, subtle warmth. (5 bars = 20 beats)
section2_duration_beats = 20
final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=54, text='Adagio cantabile'))
final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p'))

# Violin: Simple, emerging melody
part_violin.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('G4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Bar 5
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Bar 6
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('D5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2))) # Bar 7, beat 1
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 10, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2))) # Bar 7, beat 3
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Bar 8
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 16, m21.note.Rest(duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Bar 9 (transition)

# Cello: Sustained harmony, moving root
part_cello.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('G2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('A2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('F2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Prep for F Lydian
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 16, m21.note.Note('C3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

# Piano: Richer sustained chords (choral effect)
part_piano.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['C3', 'E3', 'G3', 'C4'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # C Major warmth
part_piano.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.chord.Chord(['G2', 'B3', 'D3', 'G3'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # G Major
part_piano.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.chord.Chord(['D3', 'F3', 'A3', 'D4'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # D minor
part_piano.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.chord.Chord(['F3', 'A3', 'C4', 'E4'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # Fmaj7, warm harmony
part_piano.insert(current_offset + 16, m21.chord.Chord(['C3', 'E3', 'G3', 'C4'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(4))) # C Major for transition

# Flute & Clarinet: Gentle sustained lines
part_flute.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('D5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('A4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 16, m21.note.Note('G4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

part_clarinet.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('B3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('A3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('F3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 16, m21.note.Note('E3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

# --- Section 3: Andante con Anima (Bars 10-13) - Purposeful, flowing, F Lydian hope ---
# Tempo: Andante con anima (72 bpm)
# Dynamics: mf to f
# F Lydian for emergent hope, preparing C Major. (4 bars = 16 beats)

final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=72, text='Andante con anima'))
final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('mf'))

# Violin: Soaring melody, exploring F Lydian
part_violin.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('F5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('A5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('B5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2))) # F Lydian #4
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 10, m21.note.Note('C6', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_violin.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('G5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

# Cello: Supporting bass line
part_cello.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('F2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('C3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('D3', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))
part_cello.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('G2', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

# Piano: "Crystalline melodies" (arpeggiated figures)
arpeggio_note_duration = m21.duration.Duration(0.5) # 8th notes for arpeggio flourishes
for i in range(4): # Four arpeggios over 4 bars
    # Arpeggio up (4 x 8th notes = 2 beats)
    if i == 0: # F Lydian
        notes = ['F3', 'A3', 'C4', 'B4'] # B natural for Lydian
        chord_notes = ['F3', 'A3', 'C4', 'B4']
    elif i == 1: # C Major
        notes = ['C4', 'E4', 'G4', 'C5']
        chord_notes = ['C4', 'E4', 'G4', 'C5']
    elif i == 2: # G Major
        notes = ['G3', 'B3', 'D4', 'G4']
        chord_notes = ['G3', 'B3', 'D4', 'G4']
    else: # G7sus4 (prepares C major)
        notes = ['G3', 'C4', 'F4', 'B4']
        chord_notes = ['G3', 'C4', 'F4', 'B4']
        
    for j, note_name in enumerate(notes):
        part_piano.insert(current_offset + (i * 4) + (j * arpeggio_note_duration.quarterLength),
                          m21.note.Note(note_name, duration=arpeggio_note_duration))
    # Sustained chord for the remaining 2 beats of the bar
    part_piano.insert(current_offset + (i * 4) + 2, m21.chord.Chord(chord_notes, duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))

# Flute & Clarinet: Harmonizing lines
part_flute.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 2, m21.note.Note('D5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 6, m21.note.Note('F5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('G5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 10, m21.note.Note('A5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_flute.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('G5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

part_clarinet.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('A4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 2, m21.note.Note('B4', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 4, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 6, m21.note.Note('D5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 8, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 10, m21.note.Note('F5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(2)))
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=m21.duration.Duration(4)))

final_stream.insert(current_offset + 12, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('f')) # Crescendo towards the end of the section
current_offset += section3_duration_beats # current_offset is now 52 (start of bar 14)

# --- Section 4: Largo Maestoso (Bars 14-16) - Pure, radiant C Major ---
# Tempo: Largo maestoso (46 bpm)
# Dynamics: f, broad, expansive
# Resolving into C Major. (3 bars = 12 beats)
section4_duration_beats = 12
final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=46, text='Largo maestoso'))
final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.key.KeySignature(0)) # Explicit C Major key signature

# All instruments resolve to a broad C Major chord, with piano/violin flourishes
final_chord_sustain_duration = m21.duration.Duration(10) # 2.5 bars
final_arpeggio_duration = m21.duration.Duration(2) # 0.5 bar

# Cello: C2-G2-C3 sustained
part_cello.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['C2', 'G2', 'C3'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(section4_duration_beats)))

# Piano: Broad C Major chord with upward flourish
part_piano.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['C3', 'E3', 'G3', 'C4', 'E4', 'G4'], duration=final_chord_sustain_duration))
# Ascending C major arpeggio for the final two beats
arpeggio_offset_final = current_offset + final_chord_sustain_duration.quarterLength
arpeggio_dur_final_note = m21.duration.Duration(0.5) # 8th note
part_piano.insert(arpeggio_offset_final, m21.note.Note('C4', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_piano.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 0.5, m21.note.Note('E4', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_piano.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 1, m21.note.Note('G4', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_piano.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 1.5, m21.note.Note('C5', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))

# Flute: G5-C6 sustained
part_flute.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['G5', 'C6'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(section4_duration_beats)))

# Clarinet: E5-G5 sustained
part_clarinet.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['E5', 'G5'], duration=m21.duration.Duration(section4_duration_beats)))

# Violin: C6 sustained, then an ascending C major arpeggio
part_violin.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C6', duration=final_chord_sustain_duration))
# Ascending C major arpeggio for the final two beats (higher octave for radiance)
part_violin.insert(arpeggio_offset_final, m21.note.Note('E5', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_violin.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 0.5, m21.note.Note('G5', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_violin.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 1, m21.note.Note('C6', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))
part_violin.insert(arpeggio_offset_final + 1.5, m21.note.Note('E6', duration=arpeggio_dur_final_note))


# Add all parts to the final stream
final_stream.append(part_violin)
final_stream.append(part_cello)
final_stream.append(part_flute)
